      • http-response

    • 1. 진행 중인 게임 결과가 없을 때, 에러
      • curl-request
      • http-request
      • http-response
    • 2. 단식 진행 중
      • curl-request
      • http-request
      • http-response
    • 3. 복식 진행 중
      • curl-request
      • http-request
      • http-response
  • 결과 입력 페이지(게임 결과 저장)
    • 1. score 값이 null일 때, 에러
      • curl-request
      • http-request
      • http-response
    • 2. score 값이 3 이상일 때, 에러
      • curl-request
      • http-request
      • http-response
    • 3. score 값이 1:1일 때, 에러
      • curl-request
      • http-request
      • http-response
    • 4. score 값의 합이 4 이상일 때, 에러
      • curl-request
      • http-request
      • http-response
    • 5. score 값이 음수일 때, 에러
      • curl-request
      • http-request
      • http-response
    • 6. score 값이 소수일 때, 에러
      • curl-request
      • http-request
      • http-response
    • 7. score 값이 숫자가 아닐 때, 에러
      • curl-request
      • http-request
      • http-response
    • 8. score 값 정상 요청
      • curl-request
      • http-request
      • http-response
    • 9. 해당 게임 score가 이미 입력돼서 데이터에도 남아있는 경우
      • curl-request
      • http-request
      • http-response
    • 10. 입력된 결과 확인
      • curl-request
      • http-request
      • http-response
  • 최근 경기 페이지
    • 1. gameId가 숫자가 아님, 에러
      • curl-request
      • http-request
      • http-response
    • 2. gameId가 음수임
      • curl-request
      • http-request
      • http-response
    • 3. gameId가 null임
      • curl-request
      • http-request
      • http-response
    • 4. count가 숫자가 아님, 에러
      • curl-request
      • http-request
      • http-response
    • 5. count가 음수임
      • curl-request
      • http-request
      • http-response
    • 6. count가 null임
      • curl-request
      • http-request
      • http-response
    • 7. count가 100 이상
      • curl-request
      • http-request
      • http-response
    • 8. status가 NOTHING같이 다른 값일 때
      • curl-request
      • http-request
      • http-response
    • 9. status가 null일 때
      • curl-request
      • http-request
      • http-response
    • 10. gameId가 1000일 때
      • curl-request
      • http-request
      • http-response

HTTP status codes

상태 코드 설명

200 OK

성공

400 Bad Request

잘못된 요청

401 Unauthorized

비인증 상태

403 Forbidden

권한 거부

404 Not Found

존재하지 않는 요청 리소스

500 Internal Server Error

서버 에러

Error status codes

상태 코드

설명

E0001

기타 에러 발생

SLOT_POST

슬롯 생성 실패

SC001

슬롯의 status가 close인 경우

SC002

유저가 이미 예약한 슬롯이 존재하는 경우

SC003

패널티 유저가 등록한 경우

SLOT_DELETE

슬롯 삭제 실패

SD001

등록되지 않은 슬롯에서 취소한 경우

SD002

매치 시작이 임박한 경우

메인 페이지

유저 정보 조회(헤더에 포함되는 정보)

curl-request

$ curl 'http://localhost:8080/pingpong/users' -i -X GET \
    -H 'Content-Type: application/json;charset=UTF-8' \
    -H 'Authorization: Bearer 0'

http-request

GET /pingpong/users HTTP/1.1
Content-Type: application/json;charset=UTF-8
Authorization: Bearer 0
Host: localhost:8080

http-response

HTTP/1.1 200 OK
Vary: Origin
Vary: Access-Control-Request-Method
Vary: Access-Control-Request-Headers
Content-Type: application/json
X-Content-Type-Options: nosniff
X-XSS-Protection: 1; mode=block
Cache-Control: no-cache, no-store, max-age=0, must-revalidate
Pragma: no-cache
Expires: 0
X-Frame-Options: DENY
Content-Length: 57

{
  "intraId" : "hakim",
  "userImageUri" : "hakim.jpg"
}

유저 정보 조회(user의 실시간 정보 조회)

curl-request

$ curl 'http://localhost:8080/pingpong/users/live' -i -X GET \
    -H 'Content-Type: application/json;charset=UTF-8' \
    -H 'Authorization: Bearer 1'

http-request

GET /pingpong/users/live HTTP/1.1
Content-Type: application/json;charset=UTF-8
Authorization: Bearer 1
Host: localhost:8080

http-response

HTTP/1.1 200 OK
Vary: Origin
Vary: Access-Control-Request-Method
Vary: Access-Control-Request-Headers
Content-Type: application/json
X-Content-Type-Options: nosniff
X-XSS-Protection: 1; mode=block
Cache-Control: no-cache, no-store, max-age=0, must-revalidate
Pragma: no-cache
Expires: 0
X-Frame-Options: DENY
Content-Length: 42

{
  "notiCount" : 0,
  "event" : "match"
}

프로필 페이지

1. 유저 정보 실패-intraId를 찾을 수 없다

curl-request

$ curl 'http://localhost:8080/pingpong/users/notFound/detail' -i -X GET \
    -H 'Content-Type: application/json;charset=UTF-8' \
    -H 'Authorization: Bearer 0'

http-request

GET /pingpong/users/notFound/detail HTTP/1.1
Content-Type: application/json;charset=UTF-8
Authorization: Bearer 0
Host: localhost:8080

http-response

HTTP/1.1 400 Bad Request
Vary: Origin
Vary: Access-Control-Request-Method
Vary: Access-Control-Request-Headers
Content-Type: application/json
X-Content-Type-Options: nosniff
X-XSS-Protection: 1; mode=block
Cache-Control: no-cache, no-store, max-age=0, must-revalidate
Pragma: no-cache
Expires: 0
X-Frame-Options: DENY
Content-Length: 66

{
  "code" : "E0001",
  "message" : "잘못된 요청입니다."
}

2. 유저 정보 조회 성공

curl-request

$ curl 'http://localhost:8080/pingpong/users/hakim/detail' -i -X GET \
    -H 'Content-Type: application/json;charset=UTF-8' \
    -H 'Authorization: Bearer 0'

http-request

GET /pingpong/users/hakim/detail HTTP/1.1
Content-Type: application/json;charset=UTF-8
Authorization: Bearer 0
Host: localhost:8080

http-response

HTTP/1.1 200 OK
Vary: Origin
Vary: Access-Control-Request-Method
Vary: Access-Control-Request-Headers
Content-Type: application/json
X-Content-Type-Options: nosniff
X-XSS-Protection: 1; mode=block
Cache-Control: no-cache, no-store, max-age=0, must-revalidate
Pragma: no-cache
Expires: 0
X-Frame-Options: DENY
Content-Length: 270

{
  "intraId" : "hakim",
  "userImageUri" : "hakim.jpg",
  "rank" : -1,
  "ppp" : 1040,
  "wins" : 0,
  "losses" : 0,
  "winRate" : 0.0,
  "racketType" : "shakehand",
  "statusMessage" : "kikikaka",
  "rivalRecord" : {
    "curUserWin" : 0,
    "targetUserWin" : 0
  }
}

1. 최근 경기 결과 그래프 보여주기 실패-intraId를 찾을 수 없다

curl-request

$ curl 'http://localhost:8080/pingpong/users/notFound/historics' -i -X GET \
    -H 'Content-Type: application/json;charset=UTF-8' \
    -H 'Authorization: Bearer 0'

http-request

GET /pingpong/users/notFound/historics HTTP/1.1
Content-Type: application/json;charset=UTF-8
Authorization: Bearer 0
Host: localhost:8080

http-response

HTTP/1.1 400 Bad Request
Vary: Origin
Vary: Access-Control-Request-Method
Vary: Access-Control-Request-Headers
Content-Type: application/json
X-Content-Type-Options: nosniff
X-XSS-Protection: 1; mode=block
Cache-Control: no-cache, no-store, max-age=0, must-revalidate
Pragma: no-cache
Expires: 0
X-Frame-Options: DENY
Content-Length: 66

{
  "code" : "E0001",
  "message" : "잘못된 요청입니다."
}

2. 최근 경기 결과 그래프 보여주기 성공

curl-request

$ curl 'http://localhost:8080/pingpong/users/hakim/historics?chartType=rank' -i -X GET \
    -H 'Content-Type: application/json;charset=UTF-8' \
    -H 'Authorization: Bearer 0'

http-request

GET /pingpong/users/hakim/historics?chartType=rank HTTP/1.1
Content-Type: application/json;charset=UTF-8
Authorization: Bearer 0
Host: localhost:8080

http-response

HTTP/1.1 200 OK
Vary: Origin
Vary: Access-Control-Request-Method
Vary: Access-Control-Request-Headers
Content-Type: application/json
X-Content-Type-Options: nosniff
X-XSS-Protection: 1; mode=block
Cache-Control: no-cache, no-store, max-age=0, must-revalidate
Pragma: no-cache
Expires: 0
X-Frame-Options: DENY
Content-Length: 89

{
  "historics" : [ {
    "ppp" : 1042,
    "date" : "2022-07-04T10:59:26.703054"
  } ]
}

프로필 업데이트

1. 프로필 수정 실패-racketType 미기입

curl-request

$ curl 'http://localhost:8080/pingpong/users/detail' -i -X PUT \
    -H 'Content-Type: application/json;charset=UTF-8' \
    -H 'Authorization: Bearer 0' \
    -d '{
  "statusMessage" : "message"
}'

http-request

PUT /pingpong/users/detail HTTP/1.1
Content-Type: application/json;charset=UTF-8
Authorization: Bearer 0
Content-Length: 33
Host: localhost:8080

{
  "statusMessage" : "message"
}

http-response

HTTP/1.1 400 Bad Request
Vary: Origin
Vary: Access-Control-Request-Method
Vary: Access-Control-Request-Headers
Content-Type: application/json
X-Content-Type-Options: nosniff
X-XSS-Protection: 1; mode=block
Cache-Control: no-cache, no-store, max-age=0, must-revalidate
Pragma: no-cache
Expires: 0
X-Frame-Options: DENY
Content-Length: 66

{
  "code" : "E0001",
  "message" : "잘못된 요청입니다."
}

2. 프로필 수정 실패-racketType 잘못 기입

curl-request

$ curl 'http://localhost:8080/pingpong/users/detail' -i -X PUT \
    -H 'Content-Type: application/json;charset=UTF-8' \
    -H 'Authorization: Bearer 0' \
    -d '{
  "racketType" : "NOTHING",
  "statusMessage" : "message"
}'

http-request

PUT /pingpong/users/detail HTTP/1.1
Content-Type: application/json;charset=UTF-8
Authorization: Bearer 0
Content-Length: 61
Host: localhost:8080

{
  "racketType" : "NOTHING",
  "statusMessage" : "message"
}

http-response

HTTP/1.1 400 Bad Request
Vary: Origin
Vary: Access-Control-Request-Method
Vary: Access-Control-Request-Headers
Content-Type: application/json
X-Content-Type-Options: nosniff
X-XSS-Protection: 1; mode=block
Cache-Control: no-cache, no-store, max-age=0, must-revalidate
Pragma: no-cache
Expires: 0
X-Frame-Options: DENY
Content-Length: 66

{
  "code" : "E0001",
  "message" : "잘못된 요청입니다."
}

4. 프로필 수정 실패-statusMessage 잘못 기입

curl-request

$ curl 'http://localhost:8080/pingpong/users/detail' -i -X PUT \
    -H 'Content-Type: application/json;charset=UTF-8' \
    -H 'Authorization: Bearer 0' \
    -d '{
  "racketType" : "penholder",
  "statusMessage" : "0123456789012345678901234567890123456789012345678901234567890123456789012345678901234567890123456789012345678901234567890123456789012345678901234567890123456789012345678901234567890123456789012345678901234567890123456789012345678901234567890123456789012345678901234567890123456789012345678901234567890123456789"
}'

http-request

PUT /pingpong/users/detail HTTP/1.1
Content-Type: application/json;charset=UTF-8
Authorization: Bearer 0
Content-Length: 366
Host: localhost:8080

{
  "racketType" : "penholder",
  "statusMessage" : "0123456789012345678901234567890123456789012345678901234567890123456789012345678901234567890123456789012345678901234567890123456789012345678901234567890123456789012345678901234567890123456789012345678901234567890123456789012345678901234567890123456789012345678901234567890123456789012345678901234567890123456789"
}

http-response

HTTP/1.1 400 Bad Request
Vary: Origin
Vary: Access-Control-Request-Method
Vary: Access-Control-Request-Headers
Content-Type: application/json
X-Content-Type-Options: nosniff
X-XSS-Protection: 1; mode=block
Cache-Control: no-cache, no-store, max-age=0, must-revalidate
Pragma: no-cache
Expires: 0
X-Frame-Options: DENY
Content-Length: 66

{
  "code" : "E0001",
  "message" : "잘못된 요청입니다."
}

6. 시간 지난 슬롯 상태 보기

curl-request

$ curl 'http://localhost:8080/pingpong/match/tables/1/single' -i -X POST \
    -H 'Content-Type: application/json;charset=UTF-8' \
    -H 'Authorization: Bearer 2' \
    -d '{
  "slotId" : "111"
}'

http-request

POST /pingpong/match/tables/1/single HTTP/1.1

Authorization: Bearer 2

Host: localhost:8080

  "slotId" : "111"
}

매칭 슬롯 입장 에러(악의 접근)

1. slotId가 -1일 때

curl-request

$ curl 'http://localhost:8080/pingpong/match/tables/1/single' -i -X POST \
    -H 'Content-Type: application/json;charset=UTF-8' \
    -H 'Authorization: Bearer 2' \
    -d '{
  "slotId" : "-1"
}'

http-request

POST /pingpong/match/tables/1/single HTTP/1.1
Content-Type: application/json;charset=UTF-8
Authorization: Bearer 2
Content-Length: 21
Host: localhost:8080

{
  "slotId" : "-1"
}

http-response

HTTP/1.1 400 Bad Request
Vary: Origin
Vary: Access-Control-Request-Method
Vary: Access-Control-Request-Headers
Content-Type: application/json
X-Content-Type-Options: nosniff
X-XSS-Protection: 1; mode=block
Cache-Control: no-cache, no-store, max-age=0, must-revalidate
Pragma: no-cache
Expires: 0
X-Frame-Options: DENY
Content-Length: 66

{
  "code" : "E0001",
  "message" : "잘못된 요청입니다."
}

2. slotId가 null일 때

curl-request

$ curl 'http://localhost:8080/pingpong/match/tables/1/single' -i -X POST \
    -H 'Content-Type: application/json;charset=UTF-8' \
    -H 'Authorization: Bearer 2'

http-request

Host: localhost:8080

http-response

Vary: Origin
Vary: Access-Control-Request-Method
Vary: Access-Control-Request-Headers

X-XSS-Protection: 1; mode=block
Cache-Control: no-cache, no-store, max-age=0, must-revalidate
Pragma: no-cache

게임 취소 aka 슬롯 퇴장(단식)

1. Imminent한 게임을 취소하려고 할 때

curl-request

$ curl 'http://localhost:8080/pingpong/match/slots/1' -i -X DELETE \
    -H 'Content-Type: application/json;charset=UTF-8' \
    -H 'Authorization: Bearer 0'

http-request

DELETE /pingpong/match/slots/1 HTTP/1.1
Content-Type: application/json;charset=UTF-8
Authorization: Bearer 0
Host: localhost:8080

http-response

HTTP/1.1 400 Bad Request
Vary: Origin
Vary: Access-Control-Request-Method
Vary: Access-Control-Request-Headers
Content-Type: application/json
X-Content-Type-Options: nosniff
X-XSS-Protection: 1; mode=block
Cache-Control: no-cache, no-store, max-age=0, must-revalidate
Pragma: no-cache
Expires: 0
X-Frame-Options: DENY
Content-Length: 66

{
  "code" : "SD002",
  "message" : "잘못된 요청입니다."
}

2. Live 게임을 취소하려고 할 때

curl-request

$ curl 'http://localhost:8080/pingpong/match/slots/1' -i -X DELETE \
    -H 'Content-Type: application/json;charset=UTF-8' \
    -H 'Authorization: Bearer 7'

Host: localhost:8080

유저 검색 페이지

1. 검색창에 k 입력시

curl-request

$ curl 'http://localhost:8080/pingpong/users/searches?q=k' -i -X GET \
    -H 'Content-Type: application/json;charset=UTF-8' \
    -H 'Authorization: Bearer 1'

Cache-Control: no-cache, no-store, max-age=0, must-revalidate

Expires: 0
X-Frame-Options: DENY
Content-Length: 70

{
  "users" : [ "hakim", "donghyuk", "jekim", "jihyukim", "daekim" ]
}

결과 입력 페이지(게임 결과 정보 찾기)

1. 진행 중인 게임 결과가 없을 때, 에러

curl-request

$ curl 'http://localhost:8080/pingpong/games/result' -i -X GET \
    -H 'Content-Type: application/json;charset=UTF-8' \
    -H 'Authorization: Bearer 3'

http-request

GET /pingpong/games/result HTTP/1.1
Content-Type: application/json;charset=UTF-8
Authorization: Bearer 3
Host: localhost:8080

http-response

HTTP/1.1 400 Bad Request
Vary: Origin
Vary: Access-Control-Request-Method
Vary: Access-Control-Request-Headers
Content-Type: application/json
X-Content-Type-Options: nosniff
X-XSS-Protection: 1; mode=block
Cache-Control: no-cache, no-store, max-age=0, must-revalidate
Pragma: no-cache
Expires: 0
X-Frame-Options: DENY
Content-Length: 66

{
  "code" : "E0001",
  "message" : "잘못된 요청입니다."
}

2. 단식 진행 중

curl-request

$ curl 'http://localhost:8080/pingpong/games/result' -i -X GET \
    -H 'Content-Type: application/json;charset=UTF-8' \
    -H 'Authorization: Bearer 0'

http-request

Content-Type: application/json;charset=UTF-8
Authorization: Bearer 0
Host: localhost:8080

http-response

HTTP/1.1 200 OK
Vary: Origin
Vary: Access-Control-Request-Method
Vary: Access-Control-Request-Headers
Content-Type: application/json
X-Content-Type-Options: nosniff
X-XSS-Protection: 1; mode=block
Cache-Control: no-cache, no-store, max-age=0, must-revalidate
Pragma: no-cache
Expires: 0
X-Frame-Options: DENY
Content-Length: 167

{
  "myTeam" : [ {
    "intraId" : "hakim",
    "userImageUri" : "hakim.jpg"
  } ],
  "enemyTeam" : [ {
    "intraId" : "nheo",
    "userImageUri" : "neho.jpg"
  } ]
}

결과 입력 페이지(게임 결과 저장)

1. score 값이 null일 때, 에러

curl-request

$ curl 'http://localhost:8080/pingpong/games/result' -i -X POST \
    -H 'Content-Type: application/json;charset=UTF-8' \
    -H 'Authorization: Bearer 2'

http-request

Content-Type: application/json;charset=UTF-8
Authorization: Bearer 2
Host: localhost:8080

http-response

Vary: Origin
Vary: Access-Control-Request-Method
Vary: Access-Control-Request-Headers
X-Content-Type-Options: nosniff
X-XSS-Protection: 1; mode=block
Cache-Control: no-cache, no-store, max-age=0, must-revalidate
Pragma: no-cache
Expires: 0
X-Frame-Options: DENY

2. score 값이 3 이상일 때, 에러

  "enemyTeamScore" : "1"

최근 경기 페이지

1. gameId가 숫자가 아님, 에러

curl-request

$ curl 'http://localhost:8080/pingpong/games?gameId=string&count=20&status=end' -i -X GET \
    -H 'Content-Type: application/json;charset=UTF-8' \
    -H 'Authorization: Bearer 0'

http-request

Content-Type: application/json;charset=UTF-8
Authorization: Bearer 0
Host: localhost:8080

Vary: Access-Control-Request-Headers

X-Content-Type-Options: nosniff

Pragma: no-cache
Expires: 0
X-Frame-Options: DENY
Content-Length: 66

  "code" : "E0001",
  "message" : "잘못된 요청입니다."

3. gameId가 null임

curl-request

$ curl 'http://localhost:8080/pingpong/games?count=20&status=end' -i -X GET \
    -H 'Content-Type: application/json;charset=UTF-8' \
    -H 'Authorization: Bearer 0'

4. count가 숫자가 아님, 에러

curl-request

$ curl 'http://localhost:8080/pingpong/games?count=string&status=end' -i -X GET \
    -H 'Content-Type: application/json;charset=UTF-8' \
    -H 'Authorization: Bearer 0'

http-request

GET /pingpong/games?count=string&status=end HTTP/1.1
Content-Type: application/json;charset=UTF-8
Authorization: Bearer 0
Host: localhost:8080

http-response

HTTP/1.1 400 Bad Request
Vary: Origin
Vary: Access-Control-Request-Method
Vary: Access-Control-Request-Headers
Content-Type: application/json
X-Content-Type-Options: nosniff
X-XSS-Protection: 1; mode=block
Cache-Control: no-cache, no-store, max-age=0, must-revalidate
Pragma: no-cache
Expires: 0
X-Frame-Options: DENY
Content-Length: 66

{
  "code" : "E0001",
  "message" : "잘못된 요청입니다."
}

7. count가 100 이상

curl-request

$ curl 'http://localhost:8080/pingpong/games?count=1234&status=end' -i -X GET \
    -H 'Content-Type: application/json;charset=UTF-8' \
    -H 'Authorization: Bearer 0'

http-request

GET /pingpong/games?count=1234&status=end HTTP/1.1
Content-Type: application/json;charset=UTF-8
Authorization: Bearer 0
Host: localhost:8080

8. status가 NOTHING같이 다른 값일 때

curl-request

$ curl 'http://localhost:8080/pingpong/games?count=20&status=NOTHING' -i -X GET \
    -H 'Content-Type: application/json;charset=UTF-8' \
    -H 'Authorization: Bearer 0'

http-request

GET /pingpong/games?count=20&status=NOTHING HTTP/1.1
Content-Type: application/json;charset=UTF-8
Authorization: Bearer 0
Host: localhost:8080

Vary: Origin

Expires: 0
X-Frame-Options: DENY
Content-Length: 12709
